   function sej_cmp() {
  var host = window.location.hostname;
  var element = document.createElement('script');
  var firstScript = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
  var url = 'https://quantcast.mgr.consensu.org'
    .concat('/choice/', 'PMu8R058rp9EU', '/', host, '/choice.js')
  var uspTries = 0;
  var uspTriesLimit = 3;
  element.async = true;
  element.type = 'text/javascript';
  element.src = url;

  firstScript.parentNode.insertBefore(element, firstScript);

  function makeStub() {
    var TCF_LOCATOR_NAME = '__tcfapiLocator';
    var queue = [];
    var win = window;
    var cmpFrame;

    function addFrame() {
      var doc = win.document;
      var otherCMP = !!(win.frames[TCF_LOCATOR_NAME]);

      if (!otherCMP) {
        if (doc.body) {
          var iframe = doc.createElement('iframe');

          iframe.style.cssText = 'display:none';
          iframe.name = TCF_LOCATOR_NAME;
          doc.body.appendChild(iframe);
        } else {
          setTimeout(addFrame, 5);
        }
      }
      return !otherCMP;
    }

    function tcfAPIHandler() {
      var gdprApplies;
      var args = arguments;

      if (!args.length) {    	  
        return queue;
      } else if (args[0] === 'setGdprApplies') {
        if (
          args.length > 3 &&
          args[2] === 2 &&
          typeof args[3] === 'boolean'
        ) {
          gdprApplies = args[3];
          if (typeof args[2] === 'function') {
            args[2]('set', true);
          }
        }
      } else if (args[0] === 'ping') {
        var retr = {
          gdprApplies: gdprApplies,
          cmpLoaded: false,
          cmpStatus: 'stub'
        };

        if (typeof args[2] === 'function') {
          args[2](retr);
        }
      } else {
        queue.push(args);
      }
      
    }

    function postMessageEventHandler(event) {
      var msgIsString = typeof event.data === 'string';
      var json = {};

      try {
        if (msgIsString) {
          json = JSON.parse(event.data);
        } else {
          json = event.data;
        }
      } catch (ignore) {}

      var payload = json.__tcfapiCall;
      
      if (payload) {
        window.__tcfapi(
          payload.command,
          payload.version,
          function(retValue, success) {
            var returnMsg = {
              __tcfapiReturn: {
                returnValue: retValue,
                success: success,
                callId: payload.callId
              }
            };
            
            if (msgIsString) {
              returnMsg = JSON.stringify(returnMsg);
            }
            event.source.postMessage(returnMsg, '*');
          },
          payload.parameter
        );
        
      }
    }

    while (win) {
      try {
        if (win.frames[TCF_LOCATOR_NAME]) {
          cmpFrame = win;
          break;
        }
      } catch (ignore) {}

      if (win === window.top) {
        break;
      }
      win = win.parent;
    }
    if (!cmpFrame) {
      addFrame();
      win.__tcfapi = tcfAPIHandler;
      win.addEventListener('message', postMessageEventHandler, false);
    }
  };

  makeStub();

  var uspStubFunction = function() {
    var arg = arguments;
    if (typeof window.__uspapi !== uspStubFunction) {
      setTimeout(function() {
        if (typeof window.__uspapi !== 'undefined') {
          window.__uspapi.apply(window.__uspapi, arg);
        }
      }, 500);
    }
  };

  var checkIfUspIsReady = function() {
    uspTries++;
    if (window.__uspapi === uspStubFunction && uspTries < uspTriesLimit) {
      console.warn('USP is not accessible');
    } else {
      clearInterval(uspInterval);
    }
  };

  if (typeof window.__uspapi === 'undefined') {
    window.__uspapi = uspStubFunction;
    var uspInterval = setInterval(checkIfUspIsReady, 6000);
  }
}

   function sej_get_ads_utm(){
        trck = 'no-referrer';
	var utm_source = sej_getUrlParameterByName('utm_source');
	
	if( utm_source === false ){
        if( typeof  document.referrer != "undefined" && document.referrer != false  ){
        	utm_source = document.referrer.substring(0, 100 );        	
        }else{
        	return 'direct';
        }
    }	

	if( utm_source !== false  && /facebook/i.test( utm_source )   ){
		trck = 'facebook';
	}
	
	if( utm_source !== false && (  /twitter/i.test( utm_source )  ||  /t\.co/i.test( utm_source )  )  ){
		trck = 'twitter';
	}
	
	if( utm_source !== false && /linkedin/i.test( utm_source )   ){
		trck = 'linkedin';
	}
	
	var utm_campaign = sej_getUrlParameterByName('utm_campaign');
	if( ( utm_campaign !== false && /facebook-ads/i.test( utm_campaign ) )  ||  ( utm_source  !== false && /facebook-ads/i.test( utm_source )) ){
		trck = 'facebook-ads';
	}

      if( utm_campaign !== false && /daily-newsletter/i.test( utm_campaign )  ){
		trck = 'daily-newsletter';
	}
	return trck; 
	
}

   var ajaxurl = 'https://www.searchenginejournal.com/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php';
            window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
                jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
                    
                    var ids = [];
                    var n   = 0;
                    $('span.abm_sej_titles').each(function(){
                        var i = 1;
                        var m = 0;
                        var items = [];
    
                        // collect data-titles
                        while( i < 6 ){
                            if( $(this).attr('data-title' + i) ){
                                items[m] = i;
                                m++;
                            }
                            i++;
                        }
    
                        // randomly decide which title to display
                        var rand = items[Math.floor(Math.random()*items.length)];
                        
                        var title = $(this).data('title' + rand);
                        var ver = $(this).data('id') + 'X' + rand;
                        $(this).attr('data-version', ver);
                        ids[n] = {ver : ver};
                        n++;
                        $(this).html(title);
                        if(rand !== 1){
                            hhref = $(this).closest('a').attr('href');
                            $(this).closest('a').attr('href',hhref + "?ver=" + ver );
                           
                            $("[data-imgid='post-anchor-"+ $(this).data('id')+"']").attr('href',hhref + "?ver=" + ver );
                            
                        }
                    })  
                    
                    if($('.sej2017_home_slider_big_title').length > 0){
                        $('.sej2017_home_slider_big_title').html($('.sej2017_home_slider_first_small_title').html());
                    }
    
    
                    $('body').delegate('.title-anchor', 'click' , function(e){
    					
                        if( $( 'span.abm_sej_titles', this ).length > 0 ){
    						var s_verclick = $( 'span.abm_sej_titles', this ).attr('data-version');
    						var s_is_click = $( 'span.abm_sej_titles', this ).attr('data-sclicked');
    						
    						$( 'span.abm_sej_titles', this ).attr('data-sclicked', '1y');
    						// check if once clicked don't send next click event
                        	if( s_verclick && !s_is_click ){
                            	$.ajax({
                        	         url: ajaxurl,
                        	         type: "POST",
                        	         datatype: "JSON",
                        	         data: {
                        	             action  : 'abm_sej_titles_clicks',
                        	             verclick : s_verclick,
                        	         },
                        	     });
                        	}
                        	
                        }
    
                    });
    
                    $('a.post-image-a').click(function(e){
                        var anchor_class = $(this).attr('data-imgid');
    
                        if( anchor_class ){
                        	anchor_class = '.'+anchor_class;
                        	
                           	 if( $( 'span', anchor_class ).length > 0 ){
    
                            	var verclick = $( 'span', anchor_class ).attr('data-version');
                                
                              	if( verclick ){
                                  	$.ajax({
                              	         url: ajaxurl,
                              	         type: "POST",
                              	         datatype: "JSON",
                              	         data: {
                              	             action  : 'abm_sej_titles_clicks',

                              	         },
                              	     });
                              	}
                              	
                          }
                        }
                    });
    
                    
                });

             <a class="sej-mobile-pimage post-image-a" data-imgid="post-anchor-399694" href="https://www.searchenginejournal.com/google-sharedarraybuffer-clarification/399694/">
              <img alt="Google Clarifies SharedArrayBuffer Email" class="b-lazy loopthumb" data-src="https://cdn.searchenginejournal.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/google-sharedarraybuffer-605611648f459-100x100.jpg" data-src2="https://cdn.searchenginejournal.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/google-sharedarraybuffer-605611648f459-200x200.jpg" height="100" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%20100%20100%22%3E%3C/svg%3E" width="100"/>

              Fire at an OVH Data Center in Europe takes down millions of sites, including WP Rocket and Imagify
             </p>

             <p>
              Here are all the latest SEO statistics you need to know: organic traffic, user behavior, industry spending, local search, Google, and more.

             </h2>
             <a class="sej-mobile-pimage post-image-a" data-imgid="post-anchor-396638" href="https://www.searchenginejournal.com/googles-john-mueller-total-number-of-backlinks-doesnt-matter/396638/">
              <img alt="Googles John Mueller: Total Number of Backlinks Doesnt Matter" class="b-lazy loopthumb" data-src="https://cdn.searchenginejournal.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/02/83f6ba60-9dfa-47cb-93ea-8b8616f8bb81-60323cfa6059f-100x100.png" data-src2="https://cdn.searchenginejournal.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/02/83f6ba60-9dfa-47cb-93ea-8b8616f8bb81-60323cfa6059f-200x200.png" height="100" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%20100%20100%22%3E%3C/svg%3E" width="100"/>
              <noscript>
               <img alt="Googles John Mueller: Total Number of Backlinks Doesnt Matter" class="loopthumb" height="100" src="https://cdn.searchenginejournal.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/02/83f6ba60-9dfa-47cb-93ea-8b8616f8bb81-60323cfa6059f-100x100.png" width="100"/>
              </noscript>
             </a>
             <div class="clearfix">
             </div>
             <p>
              Googles John Mueller says the total number of backlinks a website has doesnt matter at all to the search algorithm.
             </p>
             <div class="sej-meta-box">
              <div class="sej-paimage">
               <a href="https://www.searchenginejournal.com/author/matt-southern/">
                <img alt="Matt Southern" class="avatar b-lazy img-circle" data-src="https://cdn.searchenginejournal.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/facbdec4-0f22-4eb4-acdd-cb53e4ec2629-5fcfd5def3a99-65x65.jpeg" data-src2="https://cdn.searchenginejournal.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/facbdec4-0f22-4eb4-acdd-cb53e4ec2629-5fcfd5def3a99-130x130.jpeg" height="65" src="https://cdn.searchenginejournal.com/wp-content/themes/sej14/images/placeholder.gif" width="65"/>
                <noscript>
                 <img alt="Matt Southern" height="65" src="https://cdn.searchenginejournal.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/facbdec4-0f22-4eb4-acdd-cb53e4ec2629-5fcfd5def3a99-65x65.jpeg" width="65"/>
                </noscript>
                <span class="sej-paname">
                 Matt
                 <br/>
                 Southern
                </span>
               </a>
              </div>

             <h2 class="sej-ptitle">

              </a>
             </h2>
             <a class="sej-mobile-pimage post-image-a" data-imgid="post-anchor-213080" href="https://www.searchenginejournal.com/seo-101/why-keywords-important-seo/">
              <img alt="Why Keywords Are Still So Very Important for SEO" class="b-lazy loopthumb" data-src="https://cdn.searchenginejournal.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/seo-101-1-6037aaa4f2cfe-100x100.jpg" data-src2="https://cdn.searchenginejournal.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/seo-101-1-6037aaa4f2cfe-200x200.jpg" height="100" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%20100%20100%22%3E%3C/svg%3E" width="100"/>

    <script>
     function shasAdblock() {
            var a = document.createElement('div');
            a.innerHTML = '&nbsp;';
            a.className = 'adsbox pub_300x250 pub_300x250m pub_728x90 text-ad textAd text_ad text_ads text-ads adglare-ad-server text-ad-links';
            a.style = 'width: 1px !important; height: 1px !important; position: absolute !important; left: -10000px !important; top: -1000px !important;';
            var r = false;
            try {
                document.body.appendChild(a);
                var e = document.getElementsByClassName('adsbox')[0];
                if(e.offsetHeight === 0 || e.clientHeight === 0) r = true;
                if(window.getComputedStyle !== undefined) {
                    var tmp = window.getComputedStyle(e, null);
                    if(tmp && (tmp.getPropertyValue('display') == 'none' || tmp.getPropertyValue('visibility') == 'hidden')) r = true;
                }
                document.body.removeChild(a);
            } catch (e) {}
            return r;
        }

        if( shasAdblock() ) {
       	 is_adblocker = true;
         s_load_aax();
        }
    </script>
